\DoxyCodeLine{00112\ \textcolor{comment}{/*********************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00113\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Single\ precision\ real\ and\ complex\ packing\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00114\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ *******************************************/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00115\ \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00116\ \textcolor{comment}{/**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00117\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Symm\ packing\ is\ related\ to\ packing\ of\ symmetric\ adjoint\ blocks,\ as\ expected\ the\ packing\ leaves}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00118\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ the\ diagonal\ real,\ whatever\ is\ below\ it\ is\ copied\ from\ the\ respective\ upper\ diagonal\ element\ and\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00119\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ conjugated.\ There's\ no\ PanelMode\ available\ for\ symm\ packing.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00120\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00121\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Packing\ in\ general\ is\ supposed\ to\ leave\ the\ lhs\ block\ and\ the\ rhs\ block\ easy\ to\ be\ read\ by\ gemm\ using\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00122\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ its\ respective\ rank-\/update\ instructions.\ The\ float32/64\ versions\ are\ different\ because\ at\ this\ moment}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00123\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ the\ size\ of\ the\ accumulator\ is\ fixed\ at\ 512-\/bits\ so\ you\ can't\ have\ a\ 4x4\ accumulator\ of\ 64-\/bit\ elements.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00124\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00125\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ As\ mentioned\ earlier\ MatrixProduct\ breaks\ complex\ numbers\ into\ a\ real\ vector\ and\ a\ complex\ vector\ so\ packing\ has}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00126\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ to\ take\ that\ into\ account,\ at\ the\ moment,\ we\ run\ pack\ the\ real\ part\ and\ then\ the\ imaginary\ part,\ this\ is\ the\ main}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00127\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ reason\ why\ packing\ for\ complex\ is\ broken\ down\ into\ several\ different\ parts,\ also\ the\ reason\ why\ we\ endup\ having\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00128\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ float32/64\ and\ complex\ float32/64\ version.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00129\ \textcolor{comment}{\ **/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00404\ \textcolor{comment}{/**}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00405\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ PanelMode}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00406\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Packing\ might\ be\ called\ several\ times\ before\ being\ multiplied\ by\ gebp\_kernel,\ this\ happens\ because\ }}
\DoxyCodeLine{00407\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ on\ special\ occasions\ it\ fills\ part\ of\ block\ with\ other\ parts\ of\ the\ matrix.\ Two\ variables\ control}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00408\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ how\ PanelMode\ should\ behave:\ offset\ and\ stride.\ The\ idea\ is\ that\ those\ variables\ represent\ whatever}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00409\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ is\ going\ to\ be\ the\ real\ offset\ and\ stride\ in\ the\ future\ and\ this\ is\ what\ you\ should\ obey.\ The\ process}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00410\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ is\ to\ behave\ as\ you\ would\ with\ normal\ packing\ but\ leave\ the\ start\ of\ each\ part\ with\ the\ correct\ offset}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00411\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ and\ the\ end\ as\ well\ respecting\ the\ real\ stride\ the\ block\ will\ have.\ Gebp\ is\ aware\ of\ both\ blocks\ stride}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00412\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ and\ offset\ and\ behaves\ accordingly.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00413\ \textcolor{comment}{\ **/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00414\ }
